									<h2>Digital Marketing Course Overview</h2><p>Explore <strong>digital marketing concepts</strong>, <strong>strategies</strong>, <strong>tips</strong>, <strong>tools, </strong>and <strong>implementation</strong>, in detail, with this <strong>comprehensive classroom-based, online over Zoom, </strong>or<strong> in-house digital marketing training program </strong>that can further be tailored as per your learning requirements and/or business goals. </p><p><strong>Digital marketing is evolving</strong> at a rapid pace, and <strong>artificial intelligence </strong>is playing an increasingly important role in its development. AI can be used to <strong>automate repetitive tasks</strong>, <strong>personalize content</strong> and experiences, and <strong>optimize campaigns</strong> in real-time.</p><p>The course provides a detailed understanding of <strong>planning a website</strong>, <strong>online marketing</strong>, <strong>search engine optimization (SEO)</strong>, <strong>Google Business Profile</strong>, <strong>Google Ads campaigns</strong>, tracking the results using <strong>Google Analytics</strong>, <strong>content marketing</strong>, <strong>social media marketing, and advertising</strong>, and integrating digital marketing with AI, and automated marketing.</p><p>Learn the essentials of building an effective <strong>digital marketing strategy</strong> and its <strong>practical implementation</strong> with <strong>real-world examples</strong> with <strong>Najam Ahmed</strong>, a <strong>certified instructor </strong>with <strong>23 years of experience </strong>in the field.</p><p><a style="letter-spacing: 0px;" href="https://seointl.net/contact-us/"><b>Contact us today</b></a><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"> to find out more.</span></p>								</div>

				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
									<h2><strong>AI for Marketers &#8211; the benefits</strong></h2><p>Here&#8217;s a list of some benefits of leveraging AI that you, as a marketer, can avail:</p><ul><li><strong>Increase your revenue</strong> and <strong>reduce your cost</strong></li><li>Significantly <strong>reduce time spent on legwork</strong> and <strong>repetitive tasks</strong> using automation</li><li><strong>Personalized marketing</strong> to meet the individual needs of consumers</li><li><b>Forecast the needs</b> and <b>behaviors </b>of your customers</li><li>Get <b>actionable insights </b>from your marketing/sales/CRM data</li><li><strong>Gain the best</strong> out of your current marketing efforts</li><li><b>Get substantial ROI </b>on your advertising/marketing campaigns</li><li>Revolutionize your marketing efforts by utilizing <strong>Intelligent Marketing</strong></li></ul><p><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">While <strong>artificial intelligence (AI)</strong> is still in its early stages, it is rapidly evolving and promises to revolutionize the marketing industry. </span><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">According to a recent study, 61% of marketers believe that AI will be essential to their success in the next 1 &#8211; 2 years.</span></p><p><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"> Despite this optimism, however, adoption of AI remains slow due largely to a lack of training and education. This is a critical problem that must be addressed if the full potential of AI is to be realized. Marketing professionals need to be better informed about what AI can do and how it can be used effectively. In addition, they need to have access to tools and resources that will help them use AI to its fullest potential. Only then will we see the true transformative power of AI in the marketing world.</span></p>								</div>

									<h2>Digital Marketing Course Outline with Learning Outcome</h2>
<div class="item">
<div class="link">
<div class="list-header">
<div class="text-wrap">
<ul>
<li class="text"><strong>Digital Marketing 101</strong> | an overview of all the platforms covered by the umbrella term i.e. Digital Marketing</li>
<li><b>AI &amp; Marketing</b> | Become a next-gen marketer by understanding, leveraging, and implementing AI-powered marketing tools, strategies, and best practices. The future of marketing is now. It&#8217;s time to get started!</li>
<li><strong>27 AI-powered Tools, Strategies, and Best Practices</strong> | You will experience many AI-driven tools (including ChatGPT, Bard, Midjourney, HeyGen, Synthesia, and more) and methods that can be used to personalize customer experiences, content generation, optimize digital marketing campaigns, and automate tasks. With the help of AI, digital marketing is becoming more effective and efficient, making it an essential tool for businesses of all sizes.</li>
<li><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"><strong>AI &amp; SEO – Search Engine Optimization</strong> | Understanding 21 practical SEO strategies to bring your website to the top of Google search results with practical examples with the help of AI-powered SEO strategies, and tools.&nbsp;</span></li>
<li><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"><strong>Google Business Profile</strong> | Connecting your business with local customers by optimizing Google My Business/Google Maps listings</span></li>
<li><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"><strong>YouTube SEO</strong> | Improving your YouTube videos&#8217; visibility online</span></li>
<li><strong>AI &amp; Google Ads</strong> – Search &amp; Display Advertising Campaigns | A step-by-step practical approach for launching, monitoring, and optimizing your Google Ads campaigns. How the&nbsp;AI helps your business deliver Google Ads effectively using Smart Biddings, Automation, and bringing more conversions.&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
<li><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"><strong>AI &amp; Content Marketing</strong> | an Inbound Marketing Concepts and its Implementation. The role of AI in boosting content marketing varies from collecting and analyzing huge amounts of data to personalizing user experiences and more.</span></li>
<li><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"><strong>AI &amp; Social Media Marketing</strong> | Develop a social media marketing strategy using Blogs, Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn, Instagram, and many other tips and tools. There are a number of artificial intelligence-driven programs that can vastly improve how we use social media for marketing.</span></li>
<li><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"><strong>Social Media Advertising</strong> | How to effectively create Facebook, Instagram, and LinkedIn Paid Advertising campaigns</span></li>
<li><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"><strong>Google Analytics 4</strong> | The next generation of Analytics. Help you track your success and improve your marketing by tracking the results, and assisting you in making better marketing decisions. Google Analytics 4 enables you to measure traffic and engagement across your websites and apps.</span></li>
<li><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">Check </span><a href="#digital-marketing-course-complete-outline"><strong>the complete course outline</strong></a><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;"> here.</span></li>
</ul>

													<div class="accordion-icons">

					<div class="accordion-content">
						<p>The optimization of a Google Business Profile (formerly known as Google My Business) is a crucial step for businesses wishing to establish a robust online presence in local search results. This SEO process involves ensuring that a business&#8217;s information – including its name, address, phone number, operating hours, and services – is accurate and up-to-date. High-quality images and encouraging positive customer reviews further enhance visibility. When a business profile is optimized, it not only appears more prominently in Google Search and Maps, but it also fosters trust and credibility with potential customers, driving both online and in-person traffic.</p>					</div>

Just like traditional SEO for websites, YouTube SEO involves a combination of techniques. These include using relevant keywords in video titles, descriptions, and tags; creating high-quality, engaging content that keeps viewers watching; encouraging likes, shares, and subscriptions; and optimizing video thumbnails for click-throughs. As YouTube is the second-largest search engine in the world, effective SEO can significantly boost a video&#8217;s reach, garnering more views, engagement, and potential conversions for content creators and businesses alike.</p>					</div>

						<div class="accordion-title-wrapper">
							<h6 class="accordion-title">Google Analytics 4</h6>						</div>
													<div class="accordion-icons">
								<span
									class="accordion-icon opened-icon"><i class="fas fa-plus-circle"></i></span>
								<span
									class="accordion-icon closed-icon"><i class="fas fa-minus-circle"></i></span>
							</div>
											</div>
					<div class="accordion-content">
						<p class="whitespace-pre-wrap">Google Analytics 4 (GA4) represents the next generation of Google&#8217;s analytics platform. It collects event-based data from both websites and apps to provide a unified view of the customer journey across touchpoints. GA4 introduces new capabilities like cookieless measurement, predictive modeling without complexity, and tighter integrations with media platforms.</p><p class="whitespace-pre-wrap">At its core, GA4 is built around a new &#8220;property&#8221; concept designed for the future of measurement. Properties collect data events rather than sessions, enabling more flexible and privacy-focused analysis. GA4 properties power features like behavioral and conversion modeling to provide guidance without needing complex configurations. With GA4, analytics becomes more tightly integrated with actions on websites and apps. Overall, Google Analytics 4 aims to provide a modern analytics platform tailored for today&#8217;s multi-device world.</p>					</div>
				</div>
							<div class="accordion-section">

AI tools can analyze data to identify high-performing topics tailored to audience interests and needs. AI writing assistants boost content creation productivity. Platforms with AI also allow for personalized content optimization and distribution based on individual user data and behaviors. This results in more relevant, engaging content that resonates with each customer.</p><p class="whitespace-pre-wrap">In essence, AI enables marketers to rapidly create, tailor and deliver optimized content at scale. AI-powered chatbots provide helpful content through conversational interactions. Recommendation engines suggest additional relevant content. With capabilities like machine learning, AI content marketing efforts continuously improve through ongoing testing and data analysis. By integrating AI throughout the content marketing process, marketers can drive more effective customer experiences, engagement, conversions and growth across digital channels. AI-fueled content marketing allows for efficient, data-driven and customer-centric strategies.</p><p>This part includes:</p><ul><li>Content Marketing Ideas</li><li>Using AI Tools including ChatGPT for Content Marketing</li><li>Content Repurposing</li><li>Inbound Marketing</li><li>Discover What People are Asking about</li></ul>					</div>
				</div>
							<div class="accordion-section">
					<div class="accordion-header">
						<div class="accordion-title-wrapper">
							<h6 class="accordion-title">AI &amp; Social Media Marketing</h6>						</div>
													<div class="accordion-icons">
								<span
									class="accordion-icon opened-icon"><i class="fas fa-plus-circle"></i></span>
								<span
									class="accordion-icon closed-icon"><i class="fas fa-minus-circle"></i></span>
							</div>
											</div>
					<div class="accordion-content">
						<p>Social media provides a powerful platform for brands to engage audiences and promote content. Artificial intelligence (AI) is transforming social media marketing by enhancing how brands achieve results. AI algorithms analyze user data to develop customized audience segments and identify which content resonates. This enables precise social media targeting. Chatbots with natural language capabilities efficiently interact with customers to provide support, recommendations, and relevant content.</p><p>For organic social efforts, AI informs timing by assessing when users are most active. Additionally, computer vision identifies key objects and themes in images to craft optimized captions. In essence, artificial intelligence allows brands to connect with audiences in a more personalized, relevant and measurable way across social platforms. AI-powered social media marketing provides data-driven automation that drives smarter engagement and conversions.</p><p><strong>Social Media Marketing Strategy:</strong></p><p>We will explore the following points during social media marketing sessions:</p><ul><li><p><strong>Set Specific Goals</strong><br />&#8211; Define your social media goals and KPIs from the start so you can track progress and optimize efforts. Set SMART goals related to awareness, engagement, conversions, etc.</p></li><li><p><strong>Understand Your Target Audience </strong>&#8211; Research your audience personas on each network &#8211; their demographics, interests, needs, and behaviors. Tailor content and engagement accordingly.</p></li><li><p><strong>Track Key Performance Indicators </strong>&#8211; Identify key metrics like impressions, reach, engagement rate, conversions, etc. Analyze these KPIs regularly to measure what&#8217;s working.</p></li><li><p><strong>Choose the Right Networks </strong>&#8211; Evaluate each network based on where your audience is active and which is best suited for your goals, content types, etc. Focus efforts on one or two networks.</p></li><li><p><strong>Listen and Monitor Mentions </strong>&#8211; Use social listening tools to monitor brand mentions, sentiment, complaints, keywords, hashtags, and competitors. Respond and engage appropriately.</p></li><li><p><strong>Curate Inspiring Content </strong>&#8211; Follow influencers, brands, and news sources to curate relevant content ideas and strategies to inspire your own social campaigns.</p></li><li><p><strong>Engage Your Audience </strong>&#8211; Post content and offer incentives that spark two-way engagement with your audience &#8211; contests, Q&amp;As, user-generated content, etc.</p></li><li><p><strong>Plan an Editorial Content Calendar </strong>&#8211; <span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">Plot content categories, topics, and formats on a calendar to visualize a consistent yet varied posting strategy optimized for engagement. Also how to automate social media posting with applications such as HootSuite, Buffer, etc. </span></p></li><li><strong><span style="letter-spacing: 0px;">Start Blogging &amp; Repurposing Conten </span></strong>&#8211; Create a branded blog to generate in-depth content that humanizes your brand. Repurpose blog posts into social content.</li><li><strong>Continuously Analyze &amp; Optimize Efforts</strong> &#8211; Use analytics to identify best times, top-performing content, engagement levels, etc. Refine your strategy based on key learnings.</li></ul>					</div>
				</div>
							<div class="accordion-section">
					<div class="accordion-header">
						<div class="accordion-title-wrapper">
							<h6 class="accordion-title">Social Media Advertising</h6>						</div>
													<div class="accordion-icons">
								<span
									class="accordion-icon opened-icon"><i class="fas fa-plus-circle"></i></span>
								<span
									class="accordion-icon closed-icon"><i class="fas fa-minus-circle"></i></span>
							</div>
											</div>
					<div class="accordion-content">
						<p>AI also optimizes paid social campaigns. Machine learning algorithms apply data to adjust bids, budgets, and creative elements to improve performance and cost-efficiency. AI reviews data on past performance and tests variations to refine strategies.</p><p>You will learn how to:</p><ul><li>Launch <strong>Instagram Ads</strong> using Instagram App</li><li>To effectively target your desired audience, it&#8217;s important to understand how to properly set up and optimize campaigns in <strong>Facebook Ads Manager</strong> for both Facebook and Instagram.</li></ul>					</div>
				</div>
					</div>
						</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>
					</div>
		</section>
				<section class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-467ee7b elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-gap-beside-yes elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-column-vertical-align-stretch" data-id="467ee7b" data-element_type="section" data-e-type="section">
						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-extended">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-1d95852" data-id="1d95852" data-element_type="column" data-e-type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2887f4c elementor-widget elementor-widget-image" data-id="2887f4c" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="image.default">
